Notes:
1) Data is presented in 3 different ways: bit strings, byte strings, and ‘w’-bit length words (for the lanes).
2) Bit strings - the sequence of bits from left to right.
3) Byte strings - the bytes are left to right and the bits within the byte are right to left.
4) Words - the integer representation of the values in the lanes.
